<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schieten.html>schieten</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitschieten.html>uitschieten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to shoot out</li>
<li>to eject, to throw (out)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially of plants</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grow rapidly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">clothing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take off quickly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be extraordinary, to excel beyond the average</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitslag.html>uitslag</a> (4142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">uteslach</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitslag.html>uitslag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitslagen.html>uitslagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitslag.html>uitslagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">result</span> (e.g. sporting or exam)</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">outcome</span> (of a decision)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">rash</span></li>
<li>the act of bringing into circulation</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not protected by dikes</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the act of driving livestock into pastures</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitslag.html>uitslag</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(sport)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:afloop.html>afloop</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wedstrijd.html>wedstrijd</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:resultaat.html>resultaat</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderzoek.html>onderzoek</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:examen.html>examen</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> raadpleging)
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitslag.html>uitslag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wedstrijd.html>wedstrijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:teleurstellend.html>teleurstellend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> thuisploeg.</i> </li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitspreken.html>uitspreken</a> (5638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spreken.html>spreken</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitspreken.html>uitspreken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to pronounce</li>
<li>to announce</li>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitstekend.html>uitstekend</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitstekend.html>uitstekender</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">uitstekendst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>outstanding, excellent
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitstekende.html>uitstekende</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:oplossing.html>oplossing</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an <b>excellent</b> solution.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">  present participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitsteken.html>uitsteken</a></i></span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<ul><li><dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>Pas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitstekende.html>uitstekende</a></b> tafelpunt.</i>
<dl><dd>Watch out for that <b>protruding</b> corner of the table.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>


<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitstralen.html>uitstralen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitstraling.html>uitstraling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitstraling.html>uitstralingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitstraling.html>uitstralinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">eradiation</span></li>

***uittrekken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uittrekken.html>uittrekken</a> (6835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ûtetrecken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trekken.html>trekken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uittrekken.html>uittrekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take off (<a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trok.html>trok</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trui.html>trui</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a></b> his sweater <b>off</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull out (of), eg. a tooth</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitvallen.html>uitvallen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall out (such as hair)</li>
<li>to drop out (of a competition)</li>
<li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> functioning, to become out of order</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:sally.html>sally</a> from a besieged position</li>
<li>to turn out, result in
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nogal.html>nogal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitgevallen.html>uitgevallen</a></b>.</i>: He <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> out to be rather good.</dd></dl></li></ol>

***uitvechten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitvechten.html>uitvechten</a> (12882)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">utevechten</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vechten.html>vechten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uitvechten.html>uitvechten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reach a solution or an end through fighting; to fight it out
<ul><li><b>1799</b>, Samuel Richardson, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>Geschiedenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Karel Grandison</i> (= tr. of <i>The History of <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Charles Grandison</i>), part 4, <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> Allart (publ.), pages 314 and 315.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>Wel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meent.html>meent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:elkander.html>elkander</a> aankeeken, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zotten.html>zotten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zagen.html>zagen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:opdat.html>opdat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> zoo <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> ſpreken, den ſtrijd <a href = vnd.unilang:zouden.html>zouden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitvechten.html>uitvechten</a></b>?</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Well, and you don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> suppose that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> at one another like a pair of fools, when <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> only watching, so that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>, so to speak, would <b>fight out</b> the battle?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1988</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tijdschrift.html>Tijdschrift</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:theologie.html>theologie</a></i>, page 284.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>Onze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kennis.html>kennis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ervan.html>ervan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beperkt.html>beperkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervalst.html>vervalst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> propaganda-oorlogen <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koloniale.html>koloniale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:machten.html>machten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:uitvechten.html>uitvochten</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Our knowledge about it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seriously limited and also falsified by the propaganda wars that the colonial powers <b>fought out</b> with each other.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
